             <div class="cmp-teaser__description"> 
              <p>Reducing plastic waste is a big priority for us. As well as increasing our use of reusable materials, we’re making it easier for you to recycle our packaging. See what else we’re doing to meet our aim of Less plastic. Better plastic. No plastic.</p>
